        <script type="text/javascript">
         function essb_window799246593(oUrl, oService) {  essb_window(oUrl, oService, 283); essb_ga_tracking(oService, "both", "http://www.shibleysmiles.com/powermat-wireless-charging-system/"); }; function essb_pinterenst799246593() {essb_ga_tracking("pinterest", "both", "http://www.shibleysmiles.com/powermat-wireless-charging-system/"); essb_pinterenst(); }

        <input data-essbishovercontainer="" data-essbispostcontainer="" data-essbisposttitle="Powermat Wireless Charging System Reivew" data-essbisposturl="http://www.shibleysmiles.com/powermat-wireless-charging-system/" type="hidden" value=""/>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_-wYnCaxCjpQ/TJgUK1_aH-I/AAAAAAAACNc/_uSohhd4J_M/s1600/PowerMat.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" target="_blank">
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_-wYnCaxCjpQ/TJgUK1_aH-I/AAAAAAAACNc/_uSohhd4J_M/s320/PowerMat.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
        </p>
        <div style="text-align: center;">
         <span style="font-size: large;">
          <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Powermat-PMM-PT100-Portable-with-Powercube/dp/B002JCSAWM?ie=UTF8&amp;tag=shible-20&amp;link_code=btl&amp;camp=213689&amp;creative=392969" target="_blank">
           Powermat Portable Mat with Powercube
          </a>
          <img alt="" border="0" height="1" src="http://www.assoc-amazon.com/e/ir?t=shible-20&amp;l=btl&amp;camp=213689&amp;creative=392969&amp;o=1&amp;a=B002JCSAWM" style="border: medium none ! important; margin: 0px ! important; padding: 0px ! important;" width="1"/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <p>
         <br/>
         What is the one complaint most often heard when charging phones, blackberries, hand held games, MP3 players, etc?
         <em>
          I hate all these cords!
         </em>
         We have 6 people living in our home with a total of 5 phones, 3 Nintendo DS Lites (soon to be three my daughter is getting hers for her birthday), and 3 MP3 players. That is quite a lot of devices that need charging. I tried one of those charging stations but it was too bulky and just didnt fit the devices properly.
        </p>
        <p>
         I was so excited to be given the chance to review the
         <a href="http://www.powermat.com/" target="_blank">
          PowerMat.
         </a>
         I had heard about it and tried to win one several times in giveaways because that is just me. I like to have the newest, latest, and greatest when it comes to technology. I thought this product would be innovative and fun to review. I was not disappointed. When our shipment arrived it included the Home/Office Charger, the Portable Mat, one iPhone 3GS Receiver, 1 Nintendo DS Lite Receiver, and 2 Universal Power Cube Receivers.
        </p>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_-wYnCaxCjpQ/TJgWC-cUHAI/AAAAAAAACNk/BzG5jDMr2cs/s1600/Reviews+072.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" target="_blank">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="216" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_-wYnCaxCjpQ/TJgWC-cUHAI/AAAAAAAACNk/BzG5jDMr2cs/s400/Reviews+072.jpg" width="400"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         What I really loved about this was the sleek design and the ease of charging your devices. I personally choose not to use the iPhone Receiver only because I already have a case on my iPhone so each time I wanted to charge I had to remove my case and put it in the iPhone Receiver case. However that was easily solved with the Universal Power Cube Receiver. With the Universal Receiver you can charge almost any device, such as iPhone, LG, Sony, Samsung, and more. This turned out to be great for us because 3 of the members in the house have LG phones.
        </p>
        <p>
         We hooked up the Home/Office Mat and hid the cord behind the bar. It was great to be able to charge three devices without all the bulky cords showing, not to mention each outlet only allows for two cords unless you have an extension. The boys loved the cute little sound it makes to signal that the device is indeed being charged. You can adjust the volume and brightness of the mat as well.
        </p>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_-wYnCaxCjpQ/TJgXgW6xV8I/AAAAAAAACNs/UncSsMaEZPQ/s1600/Reviews+061.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" target="_blank">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="302" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_-wYnCaxCjpQ/TJgXgW6xV8I/AAAAAAAACNs/UncSsMaEZPQ/s400/Reviews+061.jpg" width="400"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         In this photo you can see my iPhone in its receiver case, my sons LG phone using the Universal PowerCube Receiver and also his Nintendo DS Lite in its receiver. Again I really like the sleek look of the mat. Having received the portable one as well this may be a good edition to my bedroom nightstand so I can charge my phone anywhere. The really nice thing about the portable mat is it folds up into an easy to carry case, which is perfect for those that do a lot of traveling, or even when yo go on vacation.
        </p>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_-wYnCaxCjpQ/TJgY22TsT1I/AAAAAAAACN0/YzYCDT_1Ji8/s1600/Reviews+075.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" target="_blank">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="307" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_-wYnCaxCjpQ/TJgY22TsT1I/AAAAAAAACN0/YzYCDT_1Ji8/s400/Reviews+075.jpg" width="400"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         The Home/Office Mat Retails for 99.99 with the receivers between 29.99-39.99. They can be found at many major retailers such as Best Buy, Target, Staples, and more.
        </p>
        <h3 class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <span style="color: #ff0000;">
          <strong>
           GIVEAWAY CLOSED
          </strong>
         </span>
        </h3>
        <p>
         PowerMat has graciously agreed to give one lucky winner a Home/Office PowerMat with up to three receivers that is a value of up to $220!
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <div style="text-align: center;">
         <span style="font-size: 11pt;">
          <strong>
           ************Home/Office PowerMat w/three Receivers***********
          </strong>
         </span>
        </div>
        <p>
        </p>
        <div style="text-align: left;">
         <p>
          Giveaway will end on October 8th at 11:59 pm EST.
          <span style="font-weight: normal;">
           This giveaway is open to US and Canada Only. Please make sure your email address is public on your profile or leave in your comments so I can contact you should you win.
          </span>
          The winner will be chosen by random.org and announced here as well as emailed and will have 48 hours to respond or a new winner will be chosen.
         </p>
         <div style="text-align: left;">
          Congrats to the winner!
         </div>
        </div>

        <p>

            here

Enabling your devices with Powermat Receivers allows you to Drop and Charge them on any Powermat Mat to experience wireless charging.

         <div class="comment-header">
          <div class="comment-author vcard">
           <cite class="fn">

           </cite>
           <span class="says">

           </span>
          </div>
          <div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
           <a href="http://www.shibleysmiles.com/powermat-wireless-charging-system/#comment-6005">
            September 24, 2010 at 12:30 pm
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="comment-content">
          <p>
           When a device reaches full charge, power is shut off to that device. This not only saves energy, but it also prevents overcharging of the devices battery, which can shorten battery life.
          </p>
         </div>

           <span class="says">
            says:
           </span>
          </div>
          <div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">

            October 3, 2010 at 1:48 pm
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="comment-content">
          <p>
           Powermat Wireless Charging System provides a simple, fast and efficient way to keep all of your favorite personal electronic devices charged.
          </p>
         </div>

        <li class="comment even thread-even depth-1" id="comment-9619">
         <div class="comment-header">
          <div class="comment-author vcard">
           <cite class="fn">
            michtuck
           </cite>
           <span class="says">
            says:
           </span>
          </div>
          <div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
           <a href="http://www.shibleysmiles.com/powermat-wireless-charging-system/#comment-9619">
            October 8, 2010 at 8:36 pm
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="comment-content">
          <p>
           When a device reaches full charge, power is shut off to that device.
           <br/>
           This not only saves energy, but it also prevents overcharging of the
           <br/>
           devices battery, which can shorten battery life.
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="reply">
